PDD payload audio/ragdoll audit

Goal:
  Identify which game systems enqueue objects into PDD queues.
  Specifically verify whether audio voice/playback objects or ragdoll/bone objects
  can be freed under the gheap PDD freeze guard.
  This is required before treating the 5s PDD thaw delay as the direct root cause.

======================================================================
PDD core queue functions
======================================================================
